  the</span> <span m='839110'>new</span> <span m='839420'>ones,</span> <span m='839810'>who
  will own</span> <span m='840210'>the</span> <span m='840610'>new</span> <span m='840970'>ones?</span>
  </p><p><span m='842000'>NEHA NARULA:</span> <span m='842180'>Whoever</span> <span
  m='842360'>you</span> <span m='842450'>say</span> <span m='842660'>should</span>
  <span m='842840'>own</span> <span m='842960'>the</span> <span m='843050'>new</span>
  <span m='843170'>ones</span> <span m='843940'>when--</span> <span m='845450'>a</span>
  <span m='845510'>transaction</span> <span m='846110'>consumes</span> <span m='846620'>coins</span>
  <span m='847700'>and</span> <span m='847970'>creates</span> <span m='848450'>new</span>
  <span m='848600'>ones</span> <span m='848810'>as</span> <span m='848930'>payment.</span>
  <span m='849710'>And</span> <span m='850280'>as</span> <span m='850490'>the</span>

  <span m='851060'>transaction,</span> <span m='851660'>as</span> <span m='851800'>the</span>
  <span m='851840'>spender,</span> <span m='853280'>I</span> <span m='853580'>will</span>
  <span m='853760'>decide</span> <span m='854210'>who</span> <span m='854330'>should</span>
  <span m='854450'>get</span> <span m='854570'>the</span> <span m='854660'>new</span>
  <span m='854780'>coins.</span> <span m='855170'>And</span> <span m='855290'>I'll</span>
  <span m='855350'>show</span> <span m='855500'>you</span> <span m='855570'>the</span>
  <span m='855610'>details</span> <span m='856010'>of</span> <span m='856070'>this</span>
  <span m='856430'>in</span> <span m='856520'>a</span> <span m='856580'>moment.</span>
  </p><p><span m='857326'>AUDIENCE:</span> <span m='857484'>You're</span> <span m='857642'>saying</span>

  <span m='859150'>mean</span> <span m='859830'>the</span> <span m='860240'>full</span>
  <span m='860410'>balance in the</span> <span m='860690'>account,</span> <span m='861120'>right?</span>
  </p><p><span m='862810'>NEHA NARULA:</span> <span m='862937'>No,</span> <span m='863320'>not</span>

  <span m='867820'>at</span> <span m='867970'>what's</span> <span m='868180'>happening</span>
  <span m='868450'>here.</span> <span m='868570'>Because</span> <span m='868780'>Bitcoin</span>

  <span m='869860'>track</span> <span m='870130'>of</span> <span m='870220'>balances.</span>
  <span m='871280'>So</span> <span m='871960'>let's</span> <span m='872230'>take</span>
  <span m='872440'>a</span> <span m='872500'>look</span> <span m='872740'>at</span>
  <span m='872830'>what</span> <span m='873160'>a</span> <span m='873220'>transaction</span>
  <span m='874120'>actually</span> <span m='874630'>looks</span> <span m='874870'>like.</span>
  </p><p><span m='875950'>So</span> <span m='876700'>a</span> <span m='876760'>transaction</span>

  <span m='884950'>one</span> <span m='885280'>input</span> <span m='886000'>and</span>

  <span m='948560'>So</span> <span m='948760'>this</span> <span m='949030'>is</span>

  <span m='989320'>new</span> <span m='989740'>output.</span> <span m='991660'>And</span>
  <span m='991780'>again,</span> <span m='992020'>this</span> <span m='992170'>transaction</span>
  <span m='992620'>isn't</span> <span m='992800'>just</span> <span m='992920'>one</span>

  <span m='998170'>something</span> <span m='998530'>called</span> <span m='998770'>a</span>
  <span m='998830'>scriptPubKey.</span> <span m='1000540'>What</span> <span m='1000720'>the</span>
  <span m='1000840'>scriptPubKey</span> <span m='1001710'>is,</span> <span m='1001920'>the</span>
  <span m='1002010'>scriptPubKey</span> <span m='1002880'>is</span> <span m='1003090'>a</span>
  <span m='1003150'>way</span> <span m='1003600'>of</span> <span m='1003750'>specifying</span>
  <span m='1004950'>the</span> <span m='1005040'>conditions</span> <span m='1005910'>under</span>
  <span m='1006210'>which</span> <span m='1006990'>this</span> <span m='1007200'>output</span>
  <span m='1007560'>can</span> <span m='1007740'>be</span> <span m='1007950'>redeemed.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1009860'>So</span> <span m='1011270'>in</span> <span m='1011420'>its</span>

  <span m='1018290'>I</span> <span m='1018410'>have</span> <span m='1018530'>the</span>
  <span m='1018620'>right</span> <span m='1019250'>to</span> <span m='1019370'>spend</span>
  <span m='1019700'>this.</span> <span m='1020000'>And</span> <span m='1020090'>if</span>
  <span m='1020180'>Alice</span> <span m='1020500'>is</span> <span m='1020570'>spending</span>

  <span m='1022370'>maybe</span> <span m='1022850'>the</span> <span m='1022970'>scriptPubKey</span>
  <span m='1023660'>would</span> <span m='1023840'>actually</span> <span m='1024200'>just</span>
  <span m='1024380'>be</span> <span m='1024530'>Bob's</span> <span m='1024950'>public</span>
  <span m='1025280'>key.</span> <span m='1026329'>And</span> <span m='1027230'>the</span>
  <span m='1027380'>implied</span> <span m='1027890'>meaning</span> <span m='1028190'>there</span>
  <span m='1028369'>would</span> <span m='1028550'>be,</span> <span m='1028730'>anyone</span>

  <span m='1032359'>key</span> <span m='1032599'>with that</span> <span m='1032930'>public</span>
  <span m='1033310'>key</span> <span m='1034130'>could</span> <span m='1034369'>then</span>
  <span m='1034609'>spend</span> <span m='1035150'>this</span> <span m='1035359'>output.</span>
  </p><p><span m='1038619'>One</span> <span m='1038920'>thing</span> <span m='1039250'>is</span>
  <span m='1039490'>that</span> <span m='1040750'>these</span> <span m='1041020'>two</span>
  <span m='1041200'>things</span> <span m='1041500'>together--</span> <span m='1042099'>the</span>
  <span m='1042190'>previous</span> <span m='1042609'>transaction</span> <span m='1043210'>ID</span>
  <span m='1043599'>and</span> <span m='1043720'>the</span> <span m='1043839'>index--</span>
  <span m='1044260'>serves</span> <span m='1044770'>to</span> <span m='1044950'>uniquely</span>
  <span m='1045819'>identify</span> <span m='1046660'>an</span> <span m='1046780'>output.</span>
  <span m='1047780'>So</span> <span m='1047859'>these</span> <span m='1048130'>two</span>
  <span m='1048280'>things</span> <span m='1048550'>uniquely</span> <span m='1049090'>identify</span>
  <span m='1050830'>some</span> <span m='1051010'>money</span> <span m='1051400'>to</span>
  <span m='1051580'>spend.</span> <span m='1054640'>And</span> <span m='1055240'>the</span>
  <span m='1055390'>value</span> <span m='1055990'>that's</span> <span m='1056120'>specified</span>
  <span m='1056830'>in</span> <span m='1056950'>the</span> <span m='1057070'>output</span>

  <span m='1059440'>in</span> <span m='1059560'>something</span> <span m='1059860'>called</span>
  <span m='1060100'>Satoshis,</span> <span m='1060850'>and</span> <span m='1060970'>there</span>
  <span m='1061090'>are</span> <span m='1061150'>10</span> <span m='1061390'>to</span>
  <span m='1061480'>the</span> <span m='1061630'>eighth</span> <span m='1061840'>Satoshis</span>
  <span m='1062440'>in</span> <span m='1062530'>one</span> <span m='1062680'>bitcoin.</span>
  <span m='1063430'>So</span> <span m='1063520'>the</span> <span m='1063580'>value</span>
  <span m='1063850'>doesn't</span> <span m='1064090'>have</span> <span m='1064270'>any</span>
  <span m='1064540'>decimal</span> <span m='1064900'>places</span> <span m='1065410'>in</span>
  <span m='1065530'>it.</span> <span m='1065790'>It</span> <span m='1065890'>is</span>
  <span m='1066010'>always</span> <span m='1066220'>an</span> <span m='1066310'>integer.</span>
  <span m='1067380'>And</span> <span m='1067570'>output</span> <span m='1068230'>is</span>
  <span m='1068440'>what</span> <span m='1068770'>I'm</span> <span m='1068920'>referring</span>
  <span m='1069310'>to</span> <span m='1069850'>when</span> <span m='1070060'>I</span>
  <span m='1070180'>say</span> <span m='1070390'>the</span> <span m='1070480'>word,</span>
  <span m='1070720'>coin.</span> <span m='1073090'>So,</span> <span m='1073900'>questions</span>

  <span m='1349280'>the</span> <span m='1349370'>knowledge</span> <span m='1349880'>to</span>
  <span m='1349970'>redeem.</span> </p><p><span m='1351200'>Like</span> <span m='1351410'>I</span>

  <span m='2267460'>sort</span> <span m='2267700'>of</span> <span m='2267790'>implied</span>
  <span m='2268690'>that</span> <span m='2268840'>this</span> <span m='2269050'>specified</span>
  <span m='2269830'>a</span> <span m='2269860'>key</span> <span m='2270280'>and</span>

  <span m='2274900'>I</span> <span m='2274930'>mean,</span> <span m='2275110'>I</span>
  <span m='2275170'>think</span> <span m='2275350'>this</span> <span m='2275470'>is</span>
  <span m='2275620'>really,</span> <span m='2276440'>really</span> <span m='2276760'>interesting,</span>

  <span m='2279880'>lets</span> <span m='2280090'>you</span> <span m='2280210'>specify</span>
  <span m='2280840'>lots</span> <span m='2281320'>of</span> <span m='2281440'>different</span>

  <span m='2328440'>is</span> <span m='2328650'>you</span> <span m='2328740'>want</span>

  <span m='2334320'>Bob.</span> <span m='2334980'>And</span> <span m='2335100'>so</span>

  <span m='2415090'>the</span> <span m='2415240'>input</span> <span m='2415480'>of</span>

  <span m='2422410'>So</span> <span m='2423880'>what</span> <span m='2424090'>the</span>

  <span m='2437130'>which</span> <span m='2437370'>index</span> <span m='2438210'>the</span>

  <span m='2450080'>and</span> <span m='2450470'>it</span> <span m='2450590'>puts</span>
  <span m='2450860'>them</span> <span m='2451190'>on</span> <span m='2451310'>top</span>

  <span m='2453450'>So</span> <span m='2453500'>that's</span> <span m='2453710'>the</span>
  <span m='2453800'>scriptSig</span> <span m='2454250'>up</span> <span m='2454370'>there,</span>
  <span m='2455090'>this</span> <span m='2455270'>is</span> <span m='2455390'>the</span>
  <span m='2455450'>scriptPubKey</span> <span m='2456050'>down</span> <span m='2456260'>here.</span>
  </p><p><span m='2457690'>And</span> <span m='2457820'>then</span> <span m='2457940'>it</span>

  <span m='2461990'>Bitcoin</span> <span m='2462380'>Script</span> <span m='2462710'>Interpreter,</span>
  <span m='2463580'>which</span> <span m='2463790'>is</span> <span m='2463910'>based</span>
  <span m='2464390'>on</span> <span m='2464720'>a</span> <span m='2464780'>stack</span>
  <span m='2465110'>model.</span> <span m='2465710'>So</span> <span m='2466070'>it</span>

  <span m='2469160'>It</span> <span m='2469280'>starts</span> <span m='2469610'>at</span>
  <span m='2469670'>the</span> <span m='2469730'>very</span> <span m='2469940'>top,</span>
  <span m='2470870'>and</span> <span m='2471110'>it</span> <span m='2471200'>starts</span>
  <span m='2471740'>pushing</span> <span m='2472160'>these</span> <span m='2472340'>items</span>
  <span m='2472910'>onto</span> <span m='2473240'>the</span> <span m='2473330'>stack</span>
  <span m='2474020'>and</span> <span m='2474140'>evaluating</span> <span m='2474650'>them.</span>
  <span m='2475850'>And</span> <span m='2476030'>so</span> <span m='2476240'>the</span>
  <span m='2476360'>rules</span> <span m='2476720'>are</span> <span m='2476840'>that</span>
  <span m='2476960'>constants</span> <span m='2477500'>get</span> <span m='2477650'>pushed</span>
  <span m='2477920'>onto</span> <span m='2478130'>the</span> <span m='2478190'>stack--</span>
  <span m='2478970'>and</span> <span m='2479150'>then</span> <span m='2479540'>operations--</span>
  <span m='2480380'>and</span> <span m='2480500'>these</span> <span m='2480710'>things</span>

  <span m='2486440'>these</span> <span m='2486650'>are</span> <span m='2486740'>all</span>
  <span m='2487370'>Bitcoin</span> <span m='2487640'>opcodes.</span> </p><p><span

  <span m='2490550'>rules</span> <span m='2491120'>as</span> <span m='2491240'>to</span>

  <span m='2493610'>the</span> <span m='2493700'>stack.</span> <span m='2495220'>So</span>
  <span m='2496270'>the</span> <span m='2496360'>first</span> <span m='2496600'>thing</span>
  <span m='2496680'>is</span> <span m='2496810'>a</span> <span m='2496870'>signature.</span>
  <span m='2497480'>We're</span> <span m='2497600'>going</span> <span m='2497690'>to</span>
  <span m='2497950'>pop</span> <span m='2498250'>the</span> <span m='2498340'>signature</span>
  <span m='2499090'>and</span> <span m='2499480'>push</span> <span m='2499720'>it</span>
  <span m='2499810'>onto</span> <span m='2499990'>the</span> <span m='2500080'>stack</span>
  <span m='2500440'>because</span> <span m='2500860'>it</span> <span m='2502600'>is</span>
  <span m='2502750'>a</span> <span m='2502900'>constant</span> <span m='2503920'>so</span>
  <span m='2504100'>this</span> <span m='2504280'>would</span> <span m='2504400'>be</span>
  <span m='2504610'>the</span> <span m='2504730'>signature</span> <span m='2505750'>that</span>

  </p><p><span m='2512020'>Then</span> <span m='2512410'>same</span> <span m='2512710'>thing</span>
  <span m='2512920'>with</span> <span m='2513130'>the</span> <span m='2513190'>pubkey,</span>
  <span m='2514390'>because</span> <span m='2514670'>the</span> <span m='2514730'>pubkey</span>
  <span m='2515110'>is</span> <span m='2515260'>also</span> <span m='2515560'>a</span>
  <span m='2515620'>constant.</span> <span m='2517810'>Then</span> <span m='2517890'>we're</span>
  <span m='2517980'>going</span> <span m='2518090'>to</span> <span m='2518160'>take</span>
  <span m='2518340'>this</span> <span m='2518490'>first--</span> <span m='2519420'>now,</span>
  <span m='2519670'>OK,</span> <span m='2519870'>we're</span> <span m='2519960'>done</span>
  <span m='2520140'>with</span> <span m='2520260'>constants</span> <span m='2520710'>for</span>

  <span m='2522840'>is</span> <span m='2523110'>OP_DUP.</span> <span m='2524056'>OP_DUP</span>
  <span m='2524850'>does</span> <span m='2525690'>basically</span> <span m='2526230'>exactly</span>
  <span m='2526740'>what</span> <span m='2526890'>it</span> <span m='2526980'>sounds</span>
  <span m='2527250'>like.</span> <span m='2527400'>It</span> <span m='2527490'>takes</span>
  <span m='2527790'>the</span> <span m='2527910'>thing</span> <span m='2528180'>that's</span>

  <span m='2529740'>duplicates</span> <span m='2530280'>it.</span> <span m='2531220'>So</span>

  <span m='2531690'>we</span> <span m='2531810'>consume</span> <span m='2532290'>OP_DUP</span>
